Mr. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Preface
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon Jo

1)
Our Attitude Going Forward
<Prayer> Beloved Father, today is January 19, 1975, the third Sabbath morning of the new year. We earnestly hope and wish that your infinite love, blessing, and protection may be with the gathering of unification groups spread across the world as they worship for the third time this new year. Father, as we look upon your historical providence, we understand that the current time we are in is a very serious period of crossing a significant peak. As we think about how we have longed for the day of victory that reveals your providential will, centered on one nation and one people, we realize that we, the unification groups, have a historical mission that must be offered as a complete burnt offering, united in heart and mind. 
Father, we are looking forward to your loving guidance that has led us thus far, and at the same time, we cannot help but look again to your merciful hand that has guided us while chastising us toward your intended purpose. Without you, we have no hope, we lose our purpose, and we know that we can only become a pitiful group that cannot understand our current position. 
Beloved Father, we thank you for your will that has guided us thus far. At the same time, January 19, 1975, at the headquarters church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga, Yongsan-gu, Seoul).
* This message was also published in the September 1975 issue of <Unification World>.
8 Our Attitude Going Forward
At this point, as we stand before the third seven-year course, may we become a unification group that realizes how significant each of us is in this tremendous position. 
The group that was oppressed in Korea, the group that was persecuted, the pitiful group that could not speak for themselves, is now presenting a new direction before this nation and carrying a new mission as heavenly sons and daughters. As we approach the time when we can view this from a new perspective, may each of us feel how heavy our responsibilities are going forward. 
In this time when individuals cannot act independently, we must realize that the future life and death of this nation depend on the actions of our families, churches, and the unification group. We must not merely follow the example of Jesus, who, after finishing his prayer in the Garden of Gethsemane, headed toward the path of the cross. Rather, we must fulfill our responsibilities as heavenly sons and daughters who have crossed the peak of the cross before the will of heaven and are receiving a new historical mission. Furthermore, we must become a group that embodies the hope of the Father while fulfilling our filial duties on earth and taking responsibility for the mission of historical children and historical loyalists. We earnestly hope and wish for this, Father. 
We believe that the children in East Garden are also praying for the day their parents will return to their homeland, and we hope that during this busy time, they will receive heavenly blessings. 
From now on, whether day or night, in this season of new spring, we are faced with the heavenly mission of crossing the peaks of national fortune along with global fortune, so we ask that you personally be with us in this process. 
May you move the hearts of the many people who attended the banquet at the Chosun Hotel on January 16, allowing them to realize the direction in which heaven is leading. As the young children from around the world come for the event on February 8, may this nation be allowed to convey the light of hope to their hearts. 
Until now, in a country where we could not hide our national shame, may they come to see Korea as their homeland, a place they have longed for in their faith. We earnestly hope that you will work in this way, Father. 
Also, please watch over the international mobilization team coming in April. May this period create a new atmosphere in this country, shining a new bright light upon South Korea. As a result, this nation, which could only be forsaken before heaven, may turn toward a new world of hope and become a nation remembered before you, a land of Korea that can embrace thirty million people in your love. You know well how long we have awaited this. 
For that time, we have endured the path of blood and sorrow, and we earnestly hope and wish for your blessings upon their journey. 
When one is immature and unprepared, it is acceptable to face any persecution or ridicule. However, when one matures and is able to stand before heaven, they must not become a group of concern for you, Father, failing to take responsibility on the day they stand in a central position and lead others in accordance with heavenly expectations. Each of us must realize this and become members of the Korean family who can again fulfill our national mission and our global mission in this third seven-year course. We earnestly wish for this for this nation. 
Since Jesus Christ came to this earth and shed his blood to establish the way of the cross, we have come close to two thousand years of history, and we know well that we have traversed the path of historical indemnity at the cost of much blood. 
We understand how deeply your heart aches for those you cannot abandon, Father. From now on, may we embrace them and return to heaven, centered on the nation and the world, resolving the resentment of Cain and Abel as we face the new spring day that is coming before the unification groups. We must realize that we must be extremely humble. 
We must reflect on our internal and external attitudes. We must shine with hope for tomorrow, embodying the true children who add stimulation to your heart's desire, becoming valiant and courageous as we stand as the founding heroes of your nation, receiving blessings before you and love from you, and being a group that is not lacking in being presented before all people. We earnestly hope and wish for this blessing, Father. 
We earnestly hope that you will protect us during the remaining time. This morning, we earnestly ask that your mercy and love permeate deeply into our hearts, and we offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. 
<Words> As you already know, we have completed the second seven-year course and have entered the third seven-year course. You are well aware that the upcoming period in Korea is a process of crossing from the spiritual world era to the physical national era. Therefore, you must understand that all future events will hold significant heavenly meaning during this transitional period. 
This period is one that will implant a new image before the Korean people. 
Due to the banquet held at the Chosun Hotel on the 16th, the perception of the Unification Church in Korea is changing. Additionally, we have scheduled an international joint wedding ceremony on February 8. Many young people will attend this event, and unlike the youth of this era, these young people carry a new historical mission representing heaven as they come to Korea to receive blessings. From this perspective, the event on February 8 holds tremendous historical significance. 
Following that, as you know, the international mobilization team will come to Korea in April. In this light, the banquet at the Chosun Hotel was a personal introduction by the leader, and subsequently, the young people of our Unification Church will come to Korea to show a new starting point for representing families before this nation. After that, young people from all over the world will come to this land and demonstrate their activities. 
While these events may occur in a short period, they are indeed revealing the full scope of the Unification Church and implanting a new image before the Korean people. This is how I see it from a spiritual perspective. 
I feel that this period is a time when our Unification Church must fulfill its mission to create a new atmosphere in Korea with a new attitude. From this viewpoint, we must recognize that our attitude going forward is extremely important. 
Until now, when people thought of the Unification Church, they viewed it as a church that could be freely criticized and spoken about based on rumors they had heard. However, from now on, the Unification Church will enter a dimension that cannot be viewed in such a way by society. As this situation unfolds, we must realize that external changes must accompany internal changes. 
Therefore, at this critical juncture, where external circumstances are rapidly changing, we must consider how to respond and bring about internal change. This is the task we must face. 
When we are criticized and ridiculed, it is somewhat acceptable. At that time, it means that they do not hold hope for us. Even if we make mistakes, they may think, "Well, that’s just how it is." We could have gotten by with an inadequate and immature attitude. However, as the environment changes, it becomes clear that "they must not be absent. Their path is the hope that must represent the entire chaotic society. By following them, individuals can find the path of hope, families can envision hopeful families, and this nation can find an ideal nation of a new dimension by following their path." When we think and look at it this way, there is a significant difference between our past position and the position we must take in the upcoming period. We must bring about internal change during this time. It is time to consider this. 
Whether one is a student, a parent with a family, or a church leader, everything they do will influence this nation from a new angle going forward. We must realize that we must bring about profound changes within ourselves. In this regard, we must critically reassess our internal and external aspects. 
The Unification Church must fulfill its mission as a national offering both spiritually and physically. 
True faith, as history has proven, is a path of offering. Continuing on the path of offering does not end there; this offering must connect the nation and return the fruits to heaven. That is the mission of offering. In other words, it is not enough to end with one's own salvation; there is a responsibility to connect one's own salvation to the salvation of the whole. Furthermore, there is an indemnity position to fulfill the purpose of the Lord who has made us an offering, in other words, to resolve God's grievances. 
In this light, what is our intermediary position? We are the offering. We are placed in an intermediary position. As you know, an offering must be placed before both people and God. When this offering is well presented, the person can receive blessings, and God's desires regarding that offering can be fulfilled. Standing in this important position is the offering. 
When viewed this way, we must pass through the era of personal offerings, then the era of family offerings, and then transition to the era of tribal, national, and international offerings. We should not remain in this dimension. Until now, I have stood in a spiritual offering position representing the nation, the state, or the world, but now we are entering the era of reality. 
In the past, it was sufficient to embrace the spiritual nation and take responsibility, and it was enough to fulfill responsibilities that were appropriate before God's will based on spiritual standards. However, from now on, we must transition to the era of reality. When we consider this issue, we must understand that the dimensions of the path we must take today differ significantly from those of the past. 
So, where does the Unification Church stand? In the era of spiritual standards, the physical standards were behind, but that is not the case now. We stand in a central position representing the nation in both spiritual and physical aspects. 
Therefore, the offering itself becomes an issue. Does the offering itself have historical content that can be accepted by God? This is the question. The issue is whether the offering that has grown and been prepared until now is a sincere offering in God's eyes. 
If the Unification Church is to appear before this nation and fulfill a sacrificial mission, has the Unification Church, standing in the position of the offering, left behind content that is worthy before God in the historical era we have passed through? This is the question. If such content has not been left as an offering, then there must be a blemish as an offering. There must be areas that need to be cleansed or clarified due to some flaw. 
Who will do this? This question remains. Can this be done by stepping onto the altar? No, it cannot. Before stepping onto the altar, we must prepare internally and externally to become an offering that can be deemed acceptable by heaven. We must realize this.
When viewed this way, the Unification Church must fulfill its sacrificial mission both spiritually and physically. Then, who is the priest that offers sacrifices? This is the issue. Will it be God? Or should it be someone on this earth? In this context, one might think that the teacher, who has been responsible for the spiritual realm until now, should become the priest who offers sacrifices from now on.

Of course, you all must become pure offerings yourselves, but the owner who is to offer the sacrifices must also be the same. The question is whether the one who offers the sacrifices has devoted themselves to nurturing that offering. If that offering is still not pure, then, of course, there is responsibility on the offering itself, but there is also responsibility on the part of the priest who prepared the offering. This is what I have been contemplating until now.

Therefore, what did I feel when I returned from America? I thought that upon returning to Korea, I would have to do certain things, and during this period, I must surely bring about a global spiritual fortune and connect it to a physical foundation, preparing to transcend the nation's challenges and advance into the world physically, establishing a new beginning during this urgent and serious historical period.

I could not help but reflect on what kind of person I am, who is returning to Korea with such a purpose to take responsibility for the whole by organizing both internal changes and external attitudes. Therefore, if loving the Lord your God with all your heart, all your soul, and all your mind is the first commandment, then I must also reflect on whether I have fulfilled my responsibility as a preparer who can establish this altar and nurture the offerings from that position.

Now, everything that the teacher possesses is manifested through you. The fact that prominent figures in Korea attended the banquet at the Chosun Hotel is a good opportunity for this nation to form a new connection before heaven. Bowing before heaven, reflecting on oneself in some way, and creating an external environment where one can awaken their inner self and refine their own appearance is a sign that this nation is preparing as guests for a time of offering. This cannot be overlooked.

When we see this, if those external guests, representing Korea, can bring about a change of heart and adopt an attitude to look at heaven from a new dimension, what should our Unification Church do? It is not the time to merely rejoice that our time has come. It is not the time we have been hoping for. The time we have been hoping for is different. When such a time has come, we must take responsibility from that point onward. We must take responsibility. The path we must take, looking at the purpose that can be realized and that can appear in our immediate reality, must start anew on a different level.

If we remain in the same position as before without being able to complete one purpose and move toward a new world of purpose, then the expectations of the Unification Church regarding this nation, which God desires or the teacher desires, will not be fulfilled. We must recognize that we are standing at this point today.

You must understand that internal changes must occur before external changes. When treated carelessly, one can act carelessly, but when one stands in a position where the whole has hope and can say, "Take responsibility for this. We must take responsibility for heaven and the nation's will," it is different from the past. The position is fundamentally different.

The actions of the past could not influence the whole or take responsibility. However, if the path we are taking now must influence and be responsible, it is different. In the past, we could avoid the environment, but now is not the time for that. It is not the time to evade; it is the time to walk according to a plan. Until now, excuses could be made, but from now on, excuses will not work. The truth itself must become a standard of hope and must reveal itself as a subject that replaces a center with both internal and external aspects.

In our lives, whether in family life, social life, or church life, all words, actions, and thoughts must become expressions aligned with a new purpose. You must be aware that we are at such a critical juncture.

When standing in the center, one must be able to take responsibility for everything.

So, what path must we take from now on? In the next three years, you must present a new national perspective to the nation and the people of Korea, establishing a new lifestyle system that can embody that national perspective. It must not be the same old lifestyle system that has been going on carelessly; it must stand as an unwavering center that is undoubtedly the right way.

The center is not a position that can be many. It is one. There cannot be two places where the center can reside. It is one. That one place must be where each individual stands. Based on that one standard, families must stand, tribes must stand, nations must stand, and the world must stand. If that is the case, then today, the teacher must also walk that same path. Each individual must take responsibility for determining the resolution point in their life that can replace the center.

Families must determine their resolution point as a family that can unite with that one center. Centered on national missions, centered on global missions... The body expands horizontally from individuals, but the center is one. The center is one. Similarly, you must enter that same dimension.

The Unification Church, which is opposed by the Republic of Korea, cannot take direct responsibility for the Republic of Korea. It cannot. Therefore, it is okay if there are some mistakes. However, if the Unification Church appears as the center of the Republic of Korea, then it must take responsibility.

One cannot say they will take responsibility for the good and not for the bad. What determines whether one can take responsibility or not? Taking responsibility only for good things and achieving victory is not fulfilling responsibility. When one can take responsibility for bad things, then they can be said to have completed their responsibilities as a leader. This is a different position from what is shown in our daily lives. You must understand this. Fulfilling responsibility is not simple.

The Unification Church, which must take responsibility for the world, must have a firm central posture.

So, when looking at the Republic of Korea, what position is the current Republic of Korea in? This three-year period for the Republic of Korea is extremely dangerous. This is true for any country. The world is the same. Japan is in this fate, and the United States is also in this fate. They are on the same level.

Then, who will take responsibility for this? Is there an organization or party that can take responsibility? There is not. This is something that cannot be universally concluded by anyone.

Who will take responsibility? Should the people of the world take responsibility, or if there are people of heaven, should they take responsibility? If there are people of heaven, then they must take responsibility. Then, among the religions that claim to be people of heaven, which religion will take responsibility? Can Christianity, which is to become a global religion, take responsibility? No, it cannot.

If there is an organization that serves as the central pillar of Christianity, that organization must take responsibility. There must be some group that bears the historical responsibility. When we draw this conclusion, we find that there is no such group among today's Christianity, nor among any established churches. This is a conclusion that has been tested.

So, who must take responsibility? It is the Unification Church, which could not be seen, which could not have hope, that must take this responsibility. The center, this axis, must manage all the conditions of the environment well. If one side is jagged or rough, the influence of the center does not reach properly. The environment and the center are in a relative position, but they are inextricably linked in fate.

When thinking about this, if there is an organization that can take such responsibility, or if there is a group that claims to have such content, it can only be the Unification Church. It can only be the Unification Church. If the Unification Church must take this central responsibility, then the Unification Church itself must stand firmly in the central position. This is the issue.

The Unification Churches in Korea, Japan, and the United States must be unwavering. The environment can change and grow around one axis, but that center cannot change. It must remain in one place. Therefore, the Unification Churches in Korea, Japan, and the United States are not standing in different fates.

When looking at this one axis that rotates, if fierce environments collide or strike it, can this center move? It must not move. From this perspective, who must take responsibility for all the world's responsibilities? It is not the United States. Who must take responsibility for the responsibilities of Asia? It is not Japan. Who will take responsibility for Korea? It is not the current Korean government.

Then, who must take responsibility? Those who claim to be people of heaven, who possess the central ideology, must stand firm with their roots deeply planted in the ground, especially when the environment shakes. In this light, it is more about each individual than the entire Unification Church in Korea. Each individual is the issue.

This central axis is not something that can be made by pouring molten metal like a casting. It must be a center that is deeply embedded like a thin metal wire that is gathered together. If the teacher is among you, you will connect like a drill, and as you grow thicker, you will form a steel wire. Then, it cannot be split or bent; you must establish a central posture in this shared destiny.

Thus, no matter what winds blow from the world or what environmental winds collide, it must not waver. The time has come for each of you to have that posture. No matter how much the external environment changes, no matter how catastrophic the situation becomes, you must not be swayed by it. You must reflect on whether you have established such a central posture.

And you must take responsibility for all environmental conditions. It is not just about taking responsibility for the good. It is okay if you do not take responsibility for the good. The question is whether you can take responsibility for the bad. This is the issue. Looking at Korea now, Christianity and the government are colliding. What will happen?

This is a time to test whether the center is firmly established or not. Originally, Christianity should be the center. Originally, Christianity should be the center of this nation, but Christianity has failed to take responsibility. Thus, the external current government can emerge as the center. We have entered a stage of upheaval. When thinking about this, can we take responsibility for the government and for Christianity? This is the issue. How will we influence the government, and how will we influence Christianity to break through? These complex issues are interconnected and are impacting our current stage of life, the actual position of the Unification Church. We are feeling this reality.

Today, we Unification Church members must change from the irresponsible era of yesterday. We must seriously affirm ourselves, recognizing that we stand in the center. Even if we expand environmentally, the unchangeable center itself must expand horizontally, and we must take on the mission of new development in environmental progress.

In other words, until now, if we were a seed, we must possess internal life and simply survive this winter. Just maintaining it and internally affirming that it is a living seed that has not died is sufficient. However, once spring arrives and it is planted, an internal change occurs. There may not be an external change, but internal change takes place. Here, life begins to sprout. A germ is formed, and a revolutionary struggle occurs to prepare its appearance for the environment of tomorrow.

The question is whether you have the subjective vitality to absorb and digest environmental conditions. It is essential to take on a new appearance, to have your own posture, and to absorb all environmental conditions to form a new body and reveal a new appearance. Such a process is necessary for us. This is how it should be.

All the corruption in society is not bad for those who possess life. If one can digest and absorb it, it becomes fertilizer. It can become fertilizer. Therefore, we see that by digesting this, we can turn it into a factor for development.

We are qualitatively different from established churches. We possess life elements.
There are corrupt elements over there. It is different. It must be different. The current government must also be different in this regard. Therefore, today, the Unification Church must take responsibility for the world's most difficult problems. If the Unification Church itself desires to be the hope of the world, it must take responsibility for the world's most difficult problems and possess the vitality to absorb and utilize them as fertilizer. I have been thinking about the issue of becoming such a Unification Church. Can it be done? Yes, it can definitely be done, and when we say that, the problem becomes simple. The problem is that it is simple.

When we think about such things, the time has changed. Aren't we entering a critical dimension from now on? We must realize this. Then, regarding whether the past was correct, if the past was not correct, we must correct it quickly. When morning comes and we suddenly open our eyes, it brightens up, and we might misunderstand that the sun is setting when we do not know the direction. We cannot distinguish whether it is evening or morning. This is not evening; it is definitely morning. It is morning. In the morning, there is a path left to go towards the new day's workplace after waking up from sleep, while in the evening, there is a path left to go towards sleep after finishing all tasks. It is a different dimension. The direction is fundamentally different.

Now is the time to open our eyes wide and grab the steering wheel properly.

22 Our Attitude Going Forward
You will not only like that the perception of the Unification Church in Korea is changing from now on. Before liking it, we must think about what we need to do. Have we recognized and can we signify that we have brought about a major change in the environment we are in? We must surely be able to say that.

It is not about escaping from the national crisis or criticizing from a position of irresponsibility; even in the midst of it, we must say, "I must take responsibility for that. It is my responsibility." You must become those who can say directly as parties involved, not as third parties criticizing the corruption of religion today, "That is my responsibility." "The chaos in society is my responsibility. All the difficulties of my neighbors are also my responsibility. I must take responsibility for all of this." Without becoming a group of the Unification Church with this new determination, it will not be possible.

That sense of responsibility will bring about changes in the surrounding environment, uniting those who did not know the center of that circle, and the united strength will transcend all corruption and emerge as a sufficient movement to overcome the difficulties of the environment, allowing this nation to be reborn and the social climate to be innovated. Who will do that? It will not be God, nor will it be this nation. We must be the ones to play that role. You must think about this.

You hope that the time has come and say, "God, please let the time come soon." But when the time comes, what will you do? "When the time comes, since we have suffered and gone hungry until now, we should loosen our belts and fill our stomachs." That is not the time. It is not that kind of time.

If it is a downhill path towards a single intersection, we must descend breathlessly, and if it is an uphill path, we must charge forward. If you dance saying, "Oh, it feels good!" while going down, you will be shattered without a trace. The more you go down, the more you must prepare to go back up again. And when you go up, it is not enough to just think that you have made it; you must also prepare to go back down again. Isn't that so? This is the same as riding a sled on a high mountain ridge. If you go down and say, "Oh, this feels good!" while closing your eyes, you will end up in disaster.

You must pass through the valley and gain the ability to rebound upwards by more than two-thirds. The faster, the better, but you must be able to control the direction. On a day when you can control the direction well, you can easily surpass that spot all at once. Isn't that so? If you go blindly with your eyes closed saying, "Oh, it feels good!"... If you think like this, isn't that exactly the case?

What about the teacher at the banquet, or what about the teacher on TV... Yesterday, the teacher went to Cheongpyeong, and they contacted the training center in the mountain valley of Cheongpyeong. They didn't know who Reverend Moon was, but they said they learned about him from TV and contacted him, and there was a lot of commotion. They said they liked it... But it is not something to be happy about. A terrifying situation is unfolding. Now is the time to open our eyes wide. Now is the time to grab the steering wheel properly. If we do not, a highly dangerous dimension will come before our eyes. We must feel that.

If we say we are going up a hill, we are going up a breathless hill. "Now there is only one step left..." It is a matter of an inch to cross the watershed. If you slip an inch and have to revise your plans, you will be pushed back. You must cross that inch. The question is whether you have crossed that inch. That can be a problem. Some may be going down, and some may be going up.

To take one more step forward, we must have a new awakening, and to go down further, we must also have a new awakening. Isn't it time for the whole to have a new awakening to take one more step? It is undoubtedly such a time.

At some point, there will be a time when the image of the Unification Church will change anew. There will come a time when the teacher will appear in official settings in Korea. It is not that the teacher cannot appear because he does not want to; it is because the timing of heavenly fortune is not right.

Now is the time to take on historical responsibilities.

24 Our Attitude Going Forward
From the perspective of the teacher's mission, one should not appear before the representative figures of Korea with a submissive attitude saying, "Oh, please." That does not uphold the dignity of heaven. One must fulfill their responsibilities and appear with the dignity of heaven. If I owe them a debt of gratitude, I should not stand in a position of being indebted to them; heaven does not want that. Because of that perspective, the teacher has never appeared in official settings in Korea.

To appear before the public, it must be the time when spiritual Christianity has developed into a global foundation, and this must be connected to a physical foundation in Korea as a condition for indemnity. Only then can one finally appear. Because the teacher knows this very well, the fact that he faced them for the first time in an official setting this time is a historical dimension. It has reached a historical dimension, a historical point. Is that a fact? Yes, that is a fact.

So now we have entered the stage of leading the public. "Ah! Teacher, I feel good..." No, it is from now on. It is from now on. What should someone named so-and-so from the Unification Church do? It is from now on. The prayers the teacher offered in the past were for crossing this hill, but the prayers now and the path ahead must pertain to me and the responsibilities I can fulfill.

What has been accomplished until now was for bearing historical responsibilities in the historical field, but what we must do now is for fulfilling responsibilities in the contemporary field. It is different. This side and that side are different. Fundamentally different.

So what will happen here? For the members of the Unification Church, it may be an extremely difficult time if it is difficult, and it may be an extremely easy time if it is easy. For those who have made indemnity, it may be an easy time, but for those who have not made indemnity, it will be an extremely difficult time. Do you understand? That is the time.

25 
The time of playing around in a flat place has passed. It is a decisive time. It is a decisive time. In other words, it is like the time when Jesus was negotiating with God in the Garden of Gethsemane about whether to carry the cross or not. It is the time to negotiate whether I will take on this responsibility or not. The negotiation should have already been concluded. Have you concluded it?

"What difference does it make between yesterday and today? The air is the same, the morning is the same, the environment is the same as before, the bedding is the same, the dining table is the same, and the environment is all the same, so what has changed?" you might say, but it is different. It must be different. It must be fundamentally different. This is not an irresponsible era; it has become an era of responsibility. I must become a central figure, standing as a subject, and while the entire environment may move, this center cannot move. We have already entered such a time.

One cannot establish heavenly principles with personal feelings.

Therefore, in the teacher's view, this marriage event is a good opportunity before the public... We started the second seven-year course in April. So, until April is the fortune of the second seven-year course, which is why the teacher is conducting this operation. It presents a condition for complete indemnity. This is how it is viewed. It is not just a possibility; it is indeed happening.

Now, if you were to be responsible for a university in front of a member of the Unification Church, what would you do? If you are a high school student and are told to be responsible for the entire high school, what would you do? If an employee of a certain company is told to be responsible for that company, how would you handle it when you are asked to take responsibility for the central position? That is the problem. You might say, "I'll just do it nominally," but it is not like that. If you are to be a real responsible person, what will you do?

If that is not the case, you will have to transfer your position again. No matter how much you dislike it, you will inevitably have to transfer it. 

26 Our Attitude Going Forward
No matter how many years you have believed in the Unification Church, if you do not transfer your position, you will have to do so. You must transfer it, but if you say, "Oh, I came out first... Those who dislike this are more fearful than the satanic forces that stand in opposition to fulfilling God's will. Such people must be dealt with ruthlessly. The teacher has negotiated this before heaven.

You cannot establish heavenly principles with personal feelings. Human feelings and heavenly principles cannot be combined. Human feelings lead to destruction, but heavenly principles are eternal. Therefore, based on that eternal heavenly principle, one must make judgments that remove and destroy conditions centered on an unchanging, eternal position and direction.

Then, when asked, "Have you stood in such a position to make judgments?" you should respond, "Yes, I have," and "Can it definitely be so?" "Yes, it can." That is how it should be. You have hoped for the arrival of the heavenly kingdom on earth. "Yes, let the heavenly kingdom come. Now, establish the heavenly kingdom." What will you do then? "I will just do it as I have done until now." Is that so? Absolutely not. It must change.

That is why you should not be pleased with the external changes. If you have not changed internally and established a central position, now is the time to fast and pray for repentance. You must clean up your internal organization.

"If I cannot do that, and if I realize that the time has come, please make me that kind of person again in a short time." Marriage is the manifestation of God's love through the perfection of individuality. Why do we say that we are blessed through marriage? From our principle, if Adam and Eve had not fallen and had achieved perfection, they would have entered the position of blessing. In other words, when God is the subject, the foundation from which love can be connected to the object position is ultimately achieved through perfection. In the end, perfection refers to marriage, and marriage refers to the manifestation of God's love.

Without marriage, love would not have begun in the world of humanity. This is how we see it. Ultimately, we must understand that the owner of love is not human but God. When God's love manifests among humans, that love becomes true love. Furthermore, when that heavenly true love is finally realized among humans, it becomes God's pride and joy. It is love that can be felt as divine love.

Love is not something that is achieved alone; it is achieved in a relationship of reciprocity. Therefore, for a man to achieve love, he cannot do so by himself. There must be a counterpart. There is no love that can be felt solely by a man. The same goes for women. Likewise, through the oneness of Adam and Eve, they can receive God's love by becoming one in love. From this perspective, we can understand that originally, we humans were born from God.

When the subject and object become completely one, a center of perfect love is born. We know that God is the central subject of the dual characteristics. God has both a plus and a minus aspect. In itself, the plus and minus aspects must become one. From that unified standard, the realm of peace unfolds. This is similar to body and mind; only when body and mind are completely one do we not feel any distress. This is how we see it. Therefore, within God, the plus and minus aspects must become completely one, and it is from that state that love begins.

According to our principle, when a perfect subject and object are formed, God is present. This means that a center is established. If the subject and object do not become completely one, a center cannot be established. When the subject and object are completely one and exchange with each other, this is movement. It rotates. It engages in reciprocal action. Through reciprocal action, it rotates, but this rotation must be centered around a single core.

**Message** Today, we know that humanity on this earth lives within the realm of fallen authority (the fallen world). We recognize that all of humanity lives in a world of sin as a historical fact. 

God established religions to place humanity within His will and plan. Since we are born as descendants of fallen human ancestors, it is evident that there is no way to seek God unless we overcome the peak of the fall, and we cannot even enter the kingdom of heaven. Furthermore, as beings who have fallen into a state of fallen nature, it is impossible for us to find a way to overcome the peak of the fall by ourselves. 

In overcoming the peak of the fall, we can only rely on the strength of a third party, that is, the power of another. This is the situation we find ourselves in today on this earth. Thankfully, heaven has not abandoned us and has been carrying the burden of suffering through history to help us overcome the peak of the fall, as you have learned through the principles. 

The path to elevate ourselves involves going from the position of a servant to that of a servant of servants, then to the position of a son or daughter, and then again to the position of unfallen parents, ultimately returning to the original embrace of God. This is the path of restoration. However, we must walk this path through the principles of recreation. Without this, we cannot proceed, as the teachings of the principles state. 

When creating, what is used? Initially, there was God's will.
There were thoughts of the Lord. Along with God's thoughts, there was a plan. We can understand that there was God's original intention and plan to create humanity and establish a certain human world. Therefore, no matter how much humanity has fallen, the people of God's providence today must stand in a certain position, which is to stand within God's will and plan today. It cannot be otherwise.

Then, can there be fallen humans within God's will and plan? No, there cannot be. Thus, God prepares for humans to enter into His will and plan. Centered on God's plan and will, many religions that have appeared throughout history have been established to place humans within that plan by pioneering environments and conditions.

So what is religion? It is a place of belief. What do we believe in? We believe in God. And what do we do by believing in God? By believing in God, we act according to His will. Seeking God's will is the mission of religion. God's will does not just come to pass; it is fulfilled according to God's plan.

How do we advance that plan? We go through a step-by-step process. We must pass through the position of a servant, then the position of a child, and finally the position of true parents to become true children born from true parents. Without this, we cannot face God in the Kingdom of Heaven. This is the original ideal of creation. We understand it this way.

Among religions, what kind of religions should exist? Looking at historical eras, there are primitive religions, religions of servants. There are religions that do not serve the master but instead serve the servant. What is that? It is superstitious religions like shamanism. It is a religion that serves the servant as the master. That is why the spirit world has been teaching this through various means until now.

We must go through the process of recreation. When God created humans, how did He do it? He first mixed clay and water to mold them. We must create humans. Just as there is no rebellion when you put your hand in water, the clay must also be able to comply. If it is a potter, it must be a lump of clay that can be shaped freely by the potter's will.

<Message> We ourselves are walking the path of faith. The path of faith is not one that can be walked for a lifetime or a lifetime without experiencing and realizing it.  
A believer can only become strong through experience.  
Those who listen to someone else's words and follow them want to experience whether those words are true or not through their own experiences. This is the position of humanity. Similarly, in walking the path of faith, even if we have heard the words or read the Bible, we always want to experience whether the facts we have learned are formed within ourselves.  
Moreover, the object of faith is the invisible God. Since we are centered on God in our faith, the very subject of faith becomes difficult to manifest in a way that we can clearly feel and touch in reality. Just as we see things through our five senses, we cannot feel it in a vivid way from a flat perspective. This is because we are dealing with a spiritual and formless subject, making it not easy to reach the experiential stage of that subject and ourselves.  
Experience is absolutely necessary in our faith life. Through that experience, we can know God's personality and at the same time feel what kind of internal emotional connection God has with us. We can only feel such things through the path of experience.  
Feeling happiness through our faith life and having a more ideal new hope through our faith life cannot appear without going through the process of experience.  
Looking at the history of Christianity in the past, during the 400 years of Roman persecution, the reason they could steadfastly walk the path of faith while becoming food for lions was not due to some vague position. There was a substantial experiential content that allowed them to overcome such situations. No matter how difficult the environment was, the fact that they stood in a position where that environment could not suppress them allowed them to smoothly pass through the path of martyrdom.  
When we look at the Bible, we see that whenever Peter or Paul faced difficult problems, they always prayed before Heaven, and through those prayers, Heaven gave them guidance. Whether to go somewhere or not… We know well through the Bible that there was always a foundation of internal faith life.  
The more such a foundation or tradition exists within each person, the stronger that person is. A person who has gone through such experiences can accomplish new historical tasks that no one else can. Even if the people of the world do not understand this and oppose it, the more they internally experience and feel what they have experienced, the stronger they can become in the practical world today.  
People may not believe, but they can believe in that fact from the moment they start, and even if the results do not appear, they can boldly and confidently pioneer the environment while anticipating what comes after the results. I believe this is only possible through experience. Therefore, experience is essential for us believers.  
The path of experience begins with aligning the spiritual zero point.  
You all know this well, but we need to think more about experience. Where to start? The subject is determined, but I cannot feel it. We cannot confirm it as we know through our five senses. When we think about where we can examine this, we cannot examine it from the subject. We cannot examine it from God. This must be examined from ourselves.

When we look at fallen human beings today, does the mind of a thousand people, or ten thousand people, all look the same? The foundation may be the same, but the mind itself differs according to its nature. If we draw a circle, we can draw a horizontal line and then draw a vertical line to create a 360-degree circle. Just as the degree of distinction is determined by drawing a horizontal line and a vertical line, if our minds are in a position like a circle, how we draw it becomes the issue. The horizontal line varies depending on the person drawing it. Just as our faces are different, your natures are all different.  
When drawing from the zero point to 360 degrees, the degree must be based on this standard, and the numbers accumulate. Thus, if the shape of 360 degrees and our minds are such a circle, we must recognize that the criteria for measuring those angles are all different. They are not all the same. Why is that? Just as our faces are different, our tastes are different, and our feelings are different, the horizontal and vertical lines that can draw those degrees are different. Some people are like this, while others are like that, and they are all different. The conclusion is that we must align those degrees.  
To do that, how should we proceed? We must find the zero point. Where is the zero point? It must exist. If you express the mind's nature like this, there must be a zero point. It must exist.  
When we look at the horizontal line, it is flat, but when it stands vertically, the criteria of that vertical line are all different. Then how do we align that zero point? If we go this way, it will definitely be the opposite, so we must align that zero point. When you go to a power plant, you see many meters. The Crossroads of Happiness and Misery
You have now become members of the Unification Church. You all know well that life does not always present a smooth path. As you move from your 20s to your 30s, then to your 40s, 50s, and 60s, we understand that life is gradually approaching its final moments.
Where is happiness?
When you look at it this way, when you are in your 20s, you have your parents and siblings, and you all live together, but once you reach your 30s, you start to separate. Your younger sisters get married, your older brothers move out, and then you get married too, and then your parents pass away, and it goes on like this... We experience various changes in our circumstances.
As we go through this process of life, the emotional aspects of the past gradually disperse, and although we take on new families and emotional responsibilities, it is not smooth. Sometimes parents pass away, sometimes the older brother you trusted may pass away, and sometimes the people you loved may leave, and we live surrounded by such miserable circumstances, and this is our life. Living with a husband and now having a family is also not smooth. A husband does not always do as he wishes, nor do children always do as you wish. Seeing this, we come to understand that life is full of ups and downs.
If you go fishing by the riverside or seaside and stay up all night, you can see that the waves change many times throughout the night. There are times when you wish for calm, serene, and peaceful surroundings where everything seems to be asleep, but there are also times when harshness crosses through in an instant, and during those times, we feel sadness.
When we observe this, we should understand that the weather and climate change, and that is where the beauty lies. Young people often think, "Ah, if life could be youthful forever! I don't want to grow old!" But that cannot be the case. We must learn to find beauty in change. If you only remain young, you will not appreciate the value of youth.
If you only eat delicious food all the time, you will not know the taste. There are bitter things, sweet things, salty things, spicy things, and sour things, and that is what makes it good.
Recently, when I spoke in Japanese, it didn't work out. As you know, when you speak a foreign language, it is always different from the language you learned in your homeland. Isn't that right? But now, most people understand English, right? "Yes." Raise your hand if you don't understand. No one, right?
When we see this, it is the same for you. Spring, summer, autumn, and winter change. They change, right? The beauty lies in that change. If all 24 hours were daytime, how... If you go to the North Pole, how boring would it be?
determined by me. I am the one who decides my happiness and unhappiness. So, I want you to understand that I am standing at the boundary between happiness and unhappiness. If I take one step this way, happiness comes; if I take one step that way, unhappiness comes.

Now, from this perspective, it is not easy to move from where I am standing. We must recognize that taking a moment, a single step, is extremely difficult. So, where does my movement begin? It starts from my heart, from my mind. Therefore, anyone who wants to seek victory and happiness must guard their heart. They must establish their heart and execute their resolutions. Without doing this, it is impossible to sustain a foundation of happiness.

There is no one who does not know what they must do to be happy. Is there anyone who does not know the direction they should go? Also, there is no one who does not know how they can become unhappy. But why are people unhappy, and why are they happy? Why can’t I be happy? Therefore, the issue is to add one thing to the path of happiness and to remove one thing from happiness. This is where everything is decided.

Now, do you understand?

The Starting Point of Happiness and Unhappiness

So, when does my happiness or unhappiness begin, and at what time or place does it manifest? It continues 24 hours a day. You might say, “Isn’t it different when I’m sleeping at night?” But you could die in your sleep. You could die in a fire. You could be walking down a good path, happily meeting someone, and still die on your way home. You could meet someone and hear a single word from them that could turn your entire day into unhappiness. We must recognize that there is always a knife that separates happiness and unhappiness, ready to strike at any moment.

We must understand that we are standing on such a path in life. When you entered the Unification Church, you felt good, but then you might think, “What is this? I can’t do what I want, and why do I have to do this every day? What is this evangelism? I have to go out and evangelize, doing things I never learned in my life… What does it have to do with me if that person becomes good?” There are many thoughts like this. Some might even think, “It would be better to turn back and be happy.”

7)
Drawing Closer to God
The young people gathered here are seen as the so-called leaders of the Unification Church in America, while also being people with a high level of experience. How many of you have been members for more than three years? Then, how many for more than two years! Less than two years! I understand.

To fulfill God's will, the Unification Church has come out instead of Christianity.
As you know, many members who received the blessing of 1,800 couples have attended this time. Among them, there are those who have come here with a determination to go abroad with a new global mission centered around 1975. And at the last meeting, I predicted that without establishing a new system in America, future operations in America would be impossible, so many have attended this 100-day training as preparation to create a new system. Therefore, let's talk a bit from that perspective.

We often talk about God's will. Of course, we know that God's will must be divided from the individual level to the family, tribe, nation, and all areas. If God's will had been realized from the individual through the social environment to the global environment, it would have become a world governed freely by God. Then what would that world be like? God would create individuals like this, families like this, tribes like this, nations like this, and realize His ideals.

From that perspective, there has never been a history in human history where God could do as He pleased. We know that Jesus came to this earth as the Messiah to save humanity and to fulfill God's will, but how much did Jesus work throughout his life based on the standard of wanting to fulfill God's will? From that standard, did Jesus live according to the standard that God wanted individuals to live? He did not. He could not live centered on the family, nor could he fulfill the will centered on the tribe, nation, or world. It is not difficult for us to conclude this.

Therefore, it is undeniable that Jesus, who wanted to fulfill God's will, left behind the fact that he could not realize it on this earth.

From that perspective, how much has the global Christianity that has emerged today, which follows Jesus' will, worked centered on God's will? There are countless Christians in the world today, but when we look at individuals who believe in Christianity, how many of those Christians have fulfilled the will that God desired from an ideal standard? If there are no such individuals, there cannot be families. Therefore, it concludes that such clans, churches, tribes, and nations cannot exist.

If there is such a Christianity, would God want to support it, nurture it, and gradually entrust it with global responsibilities? When we look at it, He can cooperate because it is impossible, but because it is impossible, in a limited era where such a Christianity might be needed, it cannot take responsibility when the time comes to replace it and fulfill God's will.

From this perspective, what does our Unification Church want? Since God exists, there must be a church that can align with God's will. We realized that the established churches cannot fulfill all of God's will in all areas, so we anticipated that at some point, a change would be necessary. By taking on the responsibilities needed at that time, God would want a church that could inherit and develop His will into the world. In that sense, I think the name Unification Church also came about.

The Unification Church's responsibility to fulfill God's will
Now, before we understand God's will, we need to know what kind of being God is. Without knowing that, we cannot understand His will. Today, established churches vaguely say, "God is a God of love," but that does not connect. We need to know the specific content of what kind of being that God is. The established churches say that God is "unconditionally loving," but is that really the case? Let's examine it.

When we look at this issue, we see that it is a very complex problem that is widely connected. They claim that God loves only Christians and saves only Christians, but if God is unconditionally loving, why can't others be saved? Why set such a limited boundary? Why must one believe only in Jesus? When we look at this, we cannot help but think that there is always a relative relationship between the subject and the object, between the main stream and the opposition.

So, when we talk about a government, there is a ruling party and an opposition party. Similarly, when God stands absolutely on the side of good to establish such a will, there is the opposing evil Satan.

From that perspective, it may be that only on God's side can the unconditional be established, but outside of God's side, everything is conditional. Even when looking at God Himself, if we consider that there are God's works, God's plans, God's family, and God's messengers, there cannot be a lack of differences within that realm of God.

Therefore, we cannot think that everything is the same unconditionally.

When we look at the issue of our love, we cannot deny that love expands step by step from the closest person to oneself, starting from those who are closest. Among children, they are all different. That emotional issue must also align with one's heart. Can you love someone if your husband's love does not align with your heart? There must be something that either matches or is intended to match, or it will not work emotionally. If it is already mismatched, then that is it. If you do not think about it and do not want to connect with them, how can you love? If we acknowledge that God is a personal God, the more we acknowledge it, the more we conclude that God must also love from those who are close.

Then, when it comes to the issue of closeness, there are two paths. One is the person who matches your heart, and the other is the person whose will aligns with yours.

From this perspective, if God established religion, then it must be that God's position cannot avoid addressing religion from that perspective. When you get hungry like that, God will feed you. Such things happen. The teacher has many such experiences. Out of nowhere… while walking, I get hungry, the sun is setting, and there is nowhere to go. But as I endure and sweat while walking, there are already people waiting with food prepared. Do you believe that? "Yes." They have prepared a feast, catching chickens and making rice cakes… How did that happen? Ah, last night, an ancestor appeared and said to prepare a feast because a guest would be passing by, and helped prepare it up to their work. Such things happen. You can eat until you are full, and even the townspeople, even the dogs can become fat…

If you cannot reach that hill and say, "Oh! This is hard!" and collapse, then God and everything else will be ruined. How much would God be astonished? "I was going to give you a great blessing, but you couldn’t endure and ruined it? You brat! Are you going to break a thousand years of effort?" Such things also happen. Therefore, think that what you are enduring is a trial, and that some difficulties will come…

Let’s meet God in the highest place that no one can follow.

Yes, if you go with money, think, "This is not my spending money; it is money for delivery." Think of it as money for delivery. "I am taking this to give to people." You must think that way. Then, surely, the path you take will be blessed.

How do I know that? Because as I lived like that, today, anyone would say that Moon Sun-myung is a successful person. However, at one time, I cannot express how much I longed for a room. A room. When you think of such things, do you really need money? "No." Do you really need a house? "No." Do you need land? "No." Above all, you need God. The True Form of Family

Whenever the teacher comes out, everyone gathers like this, so I think it significantly hinders studying. (Laughter) I was going to stop by briefly today, but here I am again. Since we are gathered, let me say a word...

The difference in emotional bonds of family in the East and West

Here in the West, among the current Western youth, there is a sense of the parents' feelings, or a sense of pity towards parents, or among siblings... Compared to Eastern people, I think this is quite lacking. In the East, if you look at what is taught in schools, they always teach that one must be filial to their parents. This is true from elementary school to middle and high school, and even in university, but here, it seems that such concepts are absent as soon as one enters elementary school. And even when looking at the parents here, they seem to think just like that.

So, I thought about how I perceive it: I think that in a country like America, the affluent lifestyle of Western society serves as a significant obstacle to bonding emotionally within families. Because whether it is morning, noon, or evening, there is always an abundance of food, and there are things for the mother and father. However, in Asia, because life is difficult, even if there is food, parents must feed their children, so they wait and leave some for them, and children, knowing their parents' feelings, will leave some of their food to give to their mothers. This emotional connection can always be manifested in practical life, but here, it is not so, and I think that is a significant obstacle and not a good thing.

If there is one food item, I want to eat it, but the act of sharing, giving and receiving, is habitual in the East. Here, if you want to eat, you just eat. Therefore, the relationship where parents think of me and children think of their parents has been lost due to the affluent living standards.

Even when buying clothes, in the East, one cannot just say, "Let's go buy clothes now." They already decide, "I will buy your clothes sometime," and parents work hard for months, even staying up nights to buy clothes. So, in that regard, to buy even one piece of clothing, parents often stay up several nights. Thus, even regarding one piece of clothing, we can glimpse the deep emotional bonds that Westerners cannot understand. This is not only between parents and children but also among siblings. An older brother, if there is food, even if it is time to eat, if the younger sibling is not there, there is a notion that he must give it to the younger sibling first, so we can always see that emotional bond among siblings.

Therefore, in the East, because people grow up in an environment where they care for each other in the family, we can see the deep emotional flow that binds them around the parents, but here, that is not understood. They simply think, "Mother and father gave birth to us, and they raise us just like the neighbors." Buying clothes is just something that is done, feeding is just something that is done, sending to school is just something that is done...

In places like Korea or Asia, how hard it is to go to school... For going to school, parents work harder, sweat more, and have to work night shifts in factories. Without doing this work, one cannot go to school. Thus, we can see that a deep emotional bond is formed there. Here, there is none of that.

Therefore, when talking about the feelings of parents and siblings in the East, people immediately understand. However, here, even if you talk about it, they might wonder, "Is that really so?"

So, the command for you to deploy globally by the end of April this year is because the second seven-year course ends in April, and from May, we will enter the third seven-year course. That is why we are preparing here now. The third seven-year course is a time to stand on a national basis and connect the spiritual and physical foundations to expand into a global spiritual and physical reality. This is the global starting form that the Messiah, Jesus, must fulfill. Therefore, this world mission is based on the principle of sending out those who have been blessed this time. Do you understand? "Yes."

You need to have that mindset now. "I will take responsibility for the nation and, in return, I will turn the whole world upside down." After Jesus ascended, the 120 disciples symbolized 120 nations, so it was arranged as if the Lord came to each of those 120 nations. We must carry out a global movement. Because you have been blessed, you will all be gathered close to the bride and groom, bringing the subject and object close together. Now, can these people who die come back, or can they not? "They cannot come back."

Now that we have established the conditions to conquer the global Satan, the national Satan will automatically be repelled as long as we hold on and endure. That is the plan. To do that, we will train everyone this time and make a big splash at the Yankee Stadium event... In America, we will make a big impact at Yankee Stadium. Are you confident? "Yes." I will make you do it. You must do this.

"Why did Reverend Moon hold the Madison Square Garden event and not stop? Why is he fighting again? Oh, is he going to do it at Yankee Stadium too? Has he lost his mind?" They will say. (Laughter) So, they are watching with their eyes open. "Let’s wait and see! It won’t work. It will fail." They will think that way. "Billy Graham spent 25 years building a foundation, and even with that, it is impossible; what can Reverend Moon do in just three years? Looking at it, there is no foundation. Can he do it with this?" They will think that way. But will we do it or not? "We will do it."

Our strength may be lacking, but God is alive. Believe that it can be done. By doing this, even those who want to oppose will think, "Let’s wait a little longer." That is what it is. "This time, it will automatically fail, and it will collapse automatically." They will see it that way. "Look at what Reverend Moon is doing!" Therefore, strategically, we must act this way to make them think this way.

However, once it explodes, on the day of "Wow!" their eyes will be wide open. After that, it will not be about fighting there. They plan to have 600,000 or more at the Washington event, three times the number. (Applause) "The entire population of Washington is 800,000, and you plan to mobilize all of them? This time, it will definitely fail." They will see it that way. General people think it is impossible. "This time, Reverend Moon will fail here." They think that. "Now, let’s wait and see. There’s no need to fight." They think that way. The established church is thinking that way. "Let’s wait and see. This time, Reverend Moon will fail in Washington. There’s no need to fight." They are waiting. They are in a waiting position, but when we succeed, it will all be over.

If you have the belief that God exists, you can do great things globally.
Now, if they try to oppose, then Reverend Moon will not be here. He will be traveling around the world with his bags packed. He will not be here. So, if all the Americans want to fight, they need an opponent. Are they going to fight you? Because of this... And then, with this data, we will make a big impact globally...

Now, if I say I’m going to England, if Reverend Moon comes to England, will the people there be interested or not? Then I will go to a big square and hold a banquet. The world will... Then what will happen? Let’s put everything in. Reverend Moon... The newspapers will report it, and everything will be done well; it won’t be done poorly. When you go out as missionaries, do you think the president of that country will want to meet the teacher or not? "I think he will." (Applause)

At that time, I will take you all with me, make you friends, and have our group love and take good care of you... I will introduce you to the missionaries. Can that happen or not? Can you do it? "Yes."

Now, if you want to oppose the American nation, go ahead and oppose. If you go around for about three years like this, "Oh, Reverend Moon! Come quickly! Come quickly!" they will say. Why? Because America needs a strong spiritual leader nationally and in every family. This goes without saying. "Even Billy Graham..." Billy Graham gathered established church members more than young people, but we are all young people. So, since the problem is from that perspective, we cannot avoid taking such risks and strategic operations; that is the teacher's perspective.

When you think about these issues, you may think they are impossible problems, but we will successfully carry them out in the first, second, and third phases. Because our faith that God is before us is strong, we know that we have the potential to do great things globally within ourselves, so we cannot avoid it.

So, you can do it in my place. You need to have this belief. At that time, if we carry out the third phase in America, we can move the public wherever we go and support and strengthen everyone. Are you confident? "Yes." You must do it with confidence. The teacher is using interpreters, but if you cannot do it in your own language, then you must die. So, this operation must be like throwing a fireball into gasoline with these 400 young people.

Now, can your mouths not be as good as the teacher's mouth? Your mouths are better than the teacher's mouth. Because you have lived well until now... The teacher has not lived well. And you speak English, right? (Laughter)

So, there is no problem. There is no problem. Therefore, think about gathering the public and doing this. Have that pride and think, "Let’s see in three years!" Let’s see in three years! Day and night, we will prepare and shoot like a machine gun! Prepare for this. Do you have that desire? "Yes." Really? "Yes." I will trust you.

At that time, think about what America will be like... What will happen in three years? No matter how rotten America is and how many hippies there are, they will inevitably be drawn to our strength. Do you want that? "Yes."

Abel must conquer Cain to rise step by step.
Now, looking at it from an Abel perspective, just like I said earlier, we must move this nation. Now, we are fighting. Here. Personal Abel, family Abel, tribal Abel, and national Abel must fight and rise, and here, we must overcome Cain for unity to happen. We must fight and win here to move to the next level. We must fight and win here to move to the next level. (Writing while speaking) You must understand this. Do you understand? "Yes."

So, do you want to do this every time, or do you want to do it all at once? Do you want to do it all at once or every time? "All at once." Are you confident you can do that? "Yes." What do you need to know? Even if you lack confidence, the teacher is currently paving the way for that representative path. Therefore, you must ride on the teacher's back. So, what the teacher has paved will be passed on to you. It will be handed over. To do that, how much do you need to trust the teacher? "......" If you trust a million, you will receive a million; if you trust ten thousand, you will receive ten thousand; if you trust greatly, you will receive greatly. Do you understand what that means? "Yes." Therefore, you must know this principle and absolutely need the teacher.

Now, what should you do? You must do this work behind the teacher, around him. If Satan attacks like this, the question is whether you can personally conquer Satan in faith or whatever.

Then, those of you who have come here are the descendants of the fallen archangel, and through the battle with this Satan, the mission of the restored archangel ends, allowing you to enter the heavenly kingdom. Thus, the history of Cain ends. Therefore, in the position of being like adopted children, you receive the same blessing and enter the heavenly kingdom. Originally, how can it be? Because there is a principled standard that could have made you Adam, but since the bloodline has changed, you are returning to the heavenly kingdom in the position of adopted children. It means that without Abel, you cannot enter heaven.

Therefore, you must understand that you share a common destiny with the teacher. Without Abel, it cannot be done. Abel and Cain must become one... That is why it is a common destiny. So, God, Adam, and the archangel become one, allowing them to enter the heavenly kingdom. This is salvation. That is where it is completed. Therefore, you have the absolute responsibility to protect the teacher, who is Abel. And I have the responsibility to take you to heaven.

Let’s fulfill Abel's responsibility and save the world.
Therefore, all of you... What the teacher is doing now is taking on Abel's responsibility to save Cain, both individually and in terms of family, tribe, nation, and world. Even if it takes a thousand or ten thousand hardships until this game is over, I will stand in a position like God, helping them and moving forward. You must surely understand that this is the position of Abel. Therefore, all the Cains that have appeared throughout history are attacking. The teacher's path is to accept all of that gladly and to go the way of digesting it. After the suffering of the nation ends, we must endure the suffering of global Christianity, and then we must overcome the suffering of the communist world; that is our path. Those who fall exhausted here cannot become Abel and cannot become Cain on heaven's side. Do you understand clearly? "Yes."

So now, if you believe in the teacher and fight globally, it will all end. This seven-year course is the final battle, and you must understand that. Now that you know this, I hope you will not be losers but victors, and that is why the teacher has given you this message. Therefore, now, depending on each of your decisions and actions, the overall value judgment will be determined.

That is why there is no time to worry about what others say. Think about it. Even if you run and run, you must decide whether to reach there in your lifetime; there is no room for other thoughts. You must know that your path is busy. You must overcome this throughout your life.

Where is heaven? Is this heaven? "No." So, knowing this clearly, now you must... Now, when you think about the Unification Church members coming together again to save America, this must be believed to be a new origin that has never existed in history, and I hope you will show a model that does not lose to foreign family members as American citizens during these three years. I will conclude my remarks. *
